This is currently called from the 'main' thread, which also\n   137→// handles 'push' requests and close - the code will eventually call the 'push' code, and it needs more mutex\n   138→// protection. Original code avoided the mutexes by doing both 'push' and 'process requests' in same thread.\n   139→func (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n   140→\tstype := v3.GetShortType(req.TypeUrl)\n   141→\tlog.Debugf(\"ADS:%s: REQ %s resources:%d nonce:%s version:%s \", stype,\n   142→\t\tcon.ID(), len(req.ResourceNames), req.ResponseNonce, req.VersionInfo)\n   143→\tif req.TypeUrl == v3.HealthInfoType {\n   144→\t\ts.handleWorkloadHealthcheck(con.proxy, req)\n   145→\t\treturn nil\n   146→\t}\n   147→\n   148→\t// For now, don't let xDS piggyback debug requests start watchers.\n   149→\tif strings.HasPrefix(req.TypeUrl, v3.DebugType) {\n   150→\t\treturn s.pushXds(con,\n   151→\t\t\t&model.WatchedResource{TypeUrl: req.TypeUrl, ResourceNames: sets.New(req.ResourceNames...)},\n   152→\t\t\t&model.PushRequest{Full: true, Push: con.proxy.LastPushContext, Forced: true})\n   153→\t}\n   154→\n   155→\tshouldRespond, delta := xds.ShouldRespond(con.proxy, con.ID(), req)\n   156→\tif !shouldRespond {\n   157→\t\treturn nil\n   158→\t}\n   159→\n   160→\trequest := &model.PushRequest{\n   161→\t\tFull:   true,\n   162→\t\tPush:   con.proxy.LastPushContext,\n   163→\t\tReason: model.NewReasonStats(model.ProxyRequest),\n   164→\n   165→\t\t// The usage of LastPushTime (rather than time.Now()), is critical here for correctness; This time\n   166→\t\t// is used by the XDS cache to determine if a entry is stale. If we use Now() with an old push context,\n   167→\t\t// we may end up overriding active cache entries with stale ones.\n   168→\t\tStart:  con.proxy.LastPushTime,\n   169→\t\tDelta:  delta,\n   170→\t\tForced: true,\n   171→\t}\n   172→\n   173→\t// SidecarScope for the proxy may not have been updated based on this pushContext.\n   174→\t// It can happen when `processRequest` comes after push context has been updated(s.initPushContext),\n   175→\t// but proxy's SidecarScope has been updated(s.computeProxyState -> SetSidecarScope) due to optimizations that skip sidecar scope\n   176→\t// computation.\n   177→\tif con.proxy.SidecarScope != nil && con.proxy.SidecarScope.Version != request.Push.PushVersion {\n   178→\t\ts.computeProxyState(con.proxy, request)\n   179→\t}\n   180→\treturn s.pushXds(con, con.proxy.GetWatchedResource(req.TypeUrl), request)\n   181→}\n   182→\n   183→// StreamAggregatedResources implements the ADS interface.\n   184→func (s *DiscoveryServer) StreamAggregatedResources(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n   185→\treturn s.Stream(stream)\n   186→}\n   187→\n   188→func (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n   189→\tif knativeEnv != \"\" && firstRequest.Load() {\n   190→\t\t// How scaling works in knative is the first request is the \"loading\" request. During\n   191→\t\t// loading request, concurrency=1. Once that request is done, concurrency is enabled.\n   192→\t\t// However, the XDS stream is long lived, so the first request would block all others. As a\n   193→\t\t// result, we should exit the first request immediately; clients will retry.\n   194→\t\tfirstRequest.Store(false)\n   195→\t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unavailable, \"server warmup not complete; try again\")\n   196→\t}\n   197→\t// Check if server is ready to accept clients and process new requests.\n   198→\t// Currently ready means caches have been synced and hence can build\n   199→\t// clusters correctly. Without this check, InitContext() call below would\n   200→\t// initialize with empty config, leading to reconnected Envoys losing\n   201→\t// configuration. This is an additional safety check inaddition to adding\n   202→\t// cachesSynced logic to readiness probe to handle cases where kube-proxy\n   203→\t// ip tables update latencies.\n   204→\t// See https://github.com/istio/istio/issues/25495.\n   205→\tif !s.IsServerReady() {\n   206→\t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unavailable, \"server is not ready to serve discovery information\")\n   207→\t}\n   208→\n   209→\tctx := stream.Context()\n   210→\tpeerAddr := \"0.0.0.0\"\n   211→\tif peerInfo, ok := peer.FromContext(ctx); ok {\n   212→\t\tpeerAddr = peerInfo.Addr.String()\n   213→\t}\n   214→\n   215→\tif err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(stream.Context()); err != nil {\n   216→\t\tlog.Warnf(\"ADS: %q exceeded rate limit: %v\", peerAddr, err)\n   217→\t\treturn status.Errorf(codes.ResourceExhausted, \"request rate limit exceeded: %v\", err)\n   218→\t}\n   219→\n   220→\tids, err := s.authenticate(ctx)\n   221→\tif err != nil {\n   222→\t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unauthenticated, err.Error())\n   223→\t}\n   224→\tif ids != nil {\n   225→\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Authenticated XDS: %v with identity %v\", peerAddr, ids)\n   226→\t} else {\n   227→\t\tlog.Debugf(\"Unauthenticated XDS: %s\", peerAddr)\n   228→\t}\n   229→\n   230→\t// InitContext returns immediately if the context was already initialized.\n   231→\ts.globalPushContext().InitContext(s.Env, nil, nil)\n   232→\tcon := newConnection(peerAddr, stream)\n   233→\tcon.ids = ids\n   234→\tcon.s = s\n   235→\treturn xds.Stream(con)\n   236→}\n   237→\n   238→// update the node associated with the connection, after receiving a packet from envoy, also adds the connection\n   239→// to the tracking map.\n   240→func (s *DiscoveryServer) initConnection(node *core.Node, con *Connection, identities []string) error {\n   241→\t// Setup the initial proxy metadata\n   242→\tproxy, err := s.initProxyMetadata(node)\n   243→\tif err != nil {\n   244→\t\treturn err\n   245→\t}\n   246→\t// Check if proxy cluster has an alias configured, if yes use that as cluster ID for this proxy.\n   247→\tif alias, exists := s.ClusterAliases[proxy.Metadata.ClusterID]; This\n   251→\t// way only new push contexts will be registered for this proxy.\n   252→\tproxy.LastPushContext = s.globalPushContext()\n   253→\t// First request so initialize connection id and start tracking it.\n   254→\tcon.SetID(connectionID(proxy.ID))\n   255→\tcon.node = node\n   256→\tcon.proxy = proxy\n   257→\tif proxy.IsZTunnel() && !features.EnableAmbient {\n   258→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"ztunnel requires PILOT_ENABLE_AMBIENT=true\")\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\t// Authorize xds clients\n   262→\tif err := s.authorize(con, identities); err != nil {\n   263→\t\treturn err\n   264→\t}\n   265→\n   266→\t// Register the connection. this allows pushes to be triggered for the proxy. Note: the timing of\n   267→\t// this and initializeProxy important. While registering for pushes *after* initialization is complete seems like\n   268→\t// a better choice, it introduces a race condition; If we complete initialization of a new push\n   269→\t// context between initializeProxy and addCon, we would not get any pushes triggered for the new\n   270→\t// push context, leading the proxy to have a stale state until the next full push.\n   271→\ts.addCon(con.ID(), con)\n   272→\t// Register that initialization is complete. This triggers to calls that it is safe to access the\n   273→\t// proxy\n   274→\tdefer con.MarkInitialized()\n   275→\n   276→\t// Complete full initialization of the proxy\n   277→\tif err := s.initializeProxy(con); err != nil {\n   278→\t\ts.closeConnection(con)\n   279→\t\treturn err\n   280→\t}\n   281→\treturn nil\n   282→}\n   283→\n   284→func (s *DiscoveryServer) closeConnection(con *Connection) {\n   285→\tif con.ID() == \"\" {\n   286→\t\treturn\n   287→\t}\n   288→\ts.removeCon(con.ID())\n   289→\ts.WorkloadEntryController.OnDisconnect(con)\n   290→}\n   291→\n   292→func connectionID(node string) string {\n   293→\tid := atomic.AddInt64(&connectionNumber, 1)\n   294→\treturn node + \"-\" + strconv.FormatInt(id, 10)\n   295→}\n   296→\n   297→// initProxyMetadata initializes just the basic metadata of a proxy. The service registries have the best access to\n   319→\t// locality information, as they can read from various sources (Node on Kubernetes, for example). They will take this\n   320→\t// information and add it to the labels. So while the proxy may not originally have these labels,\n   321→\t// it will by the time we get here (as a result of calling this after SetWorkloadLabels).\n   322→\tproxy.Locality = localityFromProxyLabels(proxy)\n   323→\tif proxy.Locality == nil {\n   324→\t\t// If there is no locality in the registry then use the one sent as part of the discovery request.\n   325→\t\t// This is not preferable as only the connected Pilot is aware of this proxies location, but it\n   326→\t\t// can still help provide some client-side Envoy context when load balancing based on location.\n   327→\t\tproxy.Locality = &core.Locality{\n   328→\t\t\tRegion:  proxy.XdsNode.Locality.GetRegion(),\n   329→\t\t\tZone:    proxy.XdsNode.Locality.GetZone(),\n   330→\t\t\tSubZone: proxy.XdsNode.Locality.GetSubZone(),\n   331→\t\t}\n   332→\t}\n   333→\t// add topology labels to proxy labels\n   334→\tproxy.Labels = labelutil.AugmentLabels(\n   335→\t\tproxy.Labels,\n   336→\t\tproxy.Metadata.ClusterID,\n   337→\t\tutil.LocalityToString(proxy.Locality),\n   338→\t\tproxy.GetNodeName(),\n   339→\t\tproxy.Metadata.Network,\n   340→\t)\n   341→}\n   342→\n   343→func localityFromProxyLabels(proxy *model.Proxy) *core.Locality {\n   344→\tregion, f1 := proxy.Labels[labelutil.LabelTopologyRegion]\n   345→\tzone, f2 := proxy.Labels[labelutil.LabelTopologyZone]\n   346→\tsubzone, f3 := proxy.Labels[label.TopologySubzone.Name]\n   347→\tif !f1 && !f2 && !f3 {\n   348→\t\t// If no labels set, we didn't find the locality from the service registry. We do support a (mostly undocumented/internal)\n   349→\t\t// label to override the locality, so respect that here as well.\n   350→\t\tlocalityLabel := pm.GetLocalityLabel(proxy.Labels)\n   351→\t\tif localityLabel != \"\" {\n   352→\t\t\treturn util.ConvertLocality(localityLabel)\n   353→\t\t}\n   354→\t\treturn nil\n   355→\t}\n   356→\treturn &core.Locality{\n   357→\t\tRegion:  region,\n   358→\t\tZone:    zone,\n   359→\t\tSubZone: subzone,\n   360→\t}\n   361→}\n   362→\n   363→// initializeProxy completes the initialization of a proxy. := proxy.LastPushContext\n   412→\tif request == nil {\n   413→\t\tshouldResetSidecarScope = true\n   414→\t} else {\n   415→\t\tpush = request.Push\n   416→\t\tif request.Forced {\n   417→\t\t\tshouldResetSidecarScope = true\n   418→\t\t}\n   419→\t\tfor conf := range request.ConfigsUpdated {\n   420→\t\t\tswitch conf.Kind {\n   421→\t\t\tcase kind.ServiceEntry, kind.DestinationRule, kind.VirtualService, kind.Sidecar:\n   422→\t\t\t\tshouldResetSidecarScope = true\n   423→\t\t\tcase kind.Gateway:\n   424→\t\t\t\tshouldResetGateway = true\n   425→\t\t\tcase 430→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   431→\t\t\t}\n   432→\t\t}\n   433→\t}\n   434→\t// compute the sidecarscope for both proxy type whenever it changes.\n   435→\tif shouldResetSidecarScope {\n resp.UnmarshalTo(&nt); err != nil {\n   155→\t\t\t\tlog.Errorf(\"failed to unmarshal name table: %v\", err)\n   156→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   157→\t\t\t}\n   158→\t\t\tia.localDNSServer.UpdateLookupTable(&nt)\n   159→\t\t\treturn nil\n   160→\t\t}\n   161→\t}\n   162→\tif ia.cfg.EnableDynamicProxyConfig && ia.secretCache != nil {\n   163→\t\tproxy.handlers[model.ProxyConfigType] = func(resp *anypb.Any) error {\n   164→\t\t\tpc := &meshconfig.ProxyConfig{}\n   165→\t\t\tif err := resp.UnmarshalTo(pc); err != nil {\n   166→\t\t\t\tlog.Errorf(\"failed to unmarshal proxy config: %v\", err)\n   167→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   168→\t\t\t}\n   169→\t\t\tcaCerts := pc.GetCaCertificatesPem()\n   170→\t\t\tlog.Debugf(\"received new certificates to add to mesh trust domain: %v\", caCerts)\n   171→\t\t\ttrustBundle := []byte{}\n   172→\t\t\tfor _, cert := range caCerts {\n   173→\t\t\t\ttrustBundle = util.AppendCertByte(trustBundle, []byte(cert))\n   174→\t\t\t}\n   175→\t\t\treturn ia.secretCache.UpdateConfigTrustBundle(trustBundle)\n   176→\t\t}\n   177→\t}\n   178→\n   179→\tproxyLog.Infof(\"Initializing with upstream address %q and cluster %q\", proxy.istiodAddress, proxy.clusterID)\n   180→\n   181→\tif err = proxy.initDownstreamServer(); err != nil {\n   182→\t\treturn nil, err\n   183→\t}\n   184→\n   185→\tif err = proxy.initIstiodDialOptions(ia); err != nil {\n   186→\t\treturn nil, err\n   187→\t}\n   188→\n   189→\tgo func() {\n   190→\t\tif err := proxy.downstreamGrpcServer.Serve(proxy.downstreamListener); err != nil {\n   191→\t\t\tlog.Errorf(\"failed to accept downstream gRPC connection %v\", err)\n   192→\t\t}\n   193→\t}()\n   194→\n   195→\tgo proxy.healthChecker.PerformApplicationHealthCheck(func(healthEvent *health.ProbeEvent) {\n   196→\t\t// Store the same response as Delta and SotW. Depending on how Envoy connects we will use one or the other.\n   197→\t\treq := &discovery.DiscoveryRequest{TypeUrl: model.HealthInfoType}\n   198→\t\tif !healthEvent.Healthy {\n   199→\t\t\treq.ErrorDetail = &google_rpc.Status{\n   200→\t\t\t\tCode:    int32(codes.Internal),\n   201→\t\t\t\tMessage: healthEvent.UnhealthyMessage,\n   202→\t\t\t}\n   203→\t\t}\n   204→\t\tproxy.sendHealthCheckRequest(req)\n   205→\t\tdeltaReq := &discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest{TypeUrl: model.HealthInfoType}\n   206→\t\tif !healthEvent.Healthy {\n   207→\t\t\tdeltaReq.ErrorDetail = &google_rpc.Status{\n   208→\t\t\t\tCode:    int32(codes.Internal),\n   209→\t\t\t\tMessage: healthEvent.UnhealthyMessage,\n   210→\t\t\t}\n   211→\t\t}\n   212→\t\tproxy.sendDeltaHealthRequest(deltaReq)\n   213→\t}, proxy.stopChan)\n   214→\n   215→\treturn proxy, nil\n   216→}\n   217→\n   218→// sendHealthCheckRequest sends a request to the currently connected proxy. Additionally, on any reconnection\n   219→// to the upstream XDS request we will resend this request.\n   220→func (p *XdsProxy) sendHealthCheckRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest) {\n   221→\tp.connectedMutex.Lock()\n   222→\t// Immediately send if we are currently connected.\n   223→\tif p.connected != nil && p.connected.requestsChan != nil {\n   224→\t\tp.connected.requestsChan.Put(req)\n   225→\t}\n   226→\t// Otherwise place it as our initial request for new connections\n   227→\tp.initialHealthRequest = req\n   228→\tp.connectedMutex.Unlock()\n   229→}\n   230→\n   231→func (p *XdsProxy) unregisterStream(c *ProxyConnection) {\n   232→\tp.connectedMutex.Lock()\n   233→\tdefer p.connectedMutex.Unlock()\n   234→\tif p.connected != nil && p.connected == c {\n   235→\t\tclose(p.connected.stopChan)\n   236→\t\tp.connected = nil\n   237→\t}\n   238→}\n   239→\n   240→func (p *XdsProxy) registerStream(c *ProxyConnection) {\n   241→\tp.connectedMutex.Lock()\n   242→\tdefer p.connectedMutex.Unlock()\n   243→\tif p.connected != nil {\n   244→\t\tproxyLog.Warnf(\"registered overlapping stream; closing previous\")\n   245→\t\tclose(p.connected.stopChan)\n   246→\t}\n   247→\tp.connected = c\n   248→}\n   249→\n   250→// ProxyConnection represents connection to downstream proxy.\n   251→type ProxyConnection struct {\n   252→\tconID              uint32\n   253→\tupstreamError      chan error\n   254→\tdownstreamError    chan error\n   255→\trequestsChan       *channels.Unbounded[*discovery.DiscoveryRequest]\n   256→\tresponsesChan      chan *discovery.DiscoveryResponse\n   257→\tdeltaRequestsChan  *channels.Unbounded[*discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest]\n   258→\tdeltaResponsesChan chan *discovery.DeltaDiscoveryResponse\n   259→\tstopChan           chan struct{}\n   260→\tdownstream         adsStream\n   261→\tupstream           DiscoveryClient\n   262→\tdownstreamDeltas   DeltaDiscoveryStream\n   263→\tupstreamDeltas     DeltaDiscoveryClient\n   264→}\n   265→\n   266→// sendRequest is a small wrapper around sending to con.requestsChan. This ensures that we do not\n   267→// block forever on\n   268→func (con *ProxyConnection) sendRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest) {\n   269→\tcon.requestsChan.Put(req)\n   270→}\n   271→\n   272→func (con *ProxyConnection) isClosed() bool {\n   273→\tselect {\n   274→\tcase <-con.stopChan:\n   275→\t\treturn true\n   276→\tdefault:\n   277→\t\treturn false\n   278→\t}\n   279→}\n   280→\n   281→type adsStream interface {\n   282→\tSend(*discovery.DiscoveryResponse) error\n   283→\tRecv() (*discovery.DiscoveryRequest, error)\n   284→\tContext() context.Context\n   285→}\n   286→\n   287→// StreamAggregatedResources is an implementation of XDS API used for proxying between Istiod and Envoy.\n   288→// Every time envoy makes a fresh connection to the agent, we reestablish a new connection to the upstream xds\n   289→// This ensures that a new connection between istiod and agent doesn't end up consuming pending messages from envoy\n   290→// as the new connection may not go to the same istiod. Vice versa case also applies.\n   291→func (p *XdsProxy) StreamAggregatedResources(downstream DiscoveryStream) error {\n   292→\tproxyLog.Debugf(\"accepted XDS connection from Envoy, forwarding to upstream XDS server\")\n   293→\treturn p.handleStream(downstream)\n   294→}\n   295→\n   296→func (p *XdsProxy) handleStream(downstream adsStream) error {\n   297→\tcon := &ProxyConnection{\n   298→\t\tconID:           connectionNumber.Inc(),\n   299→\t\tupstreamError:   make(chan error), // can be produced by recv and send\n   300→\t\tdownstreamError: make(chan error), // can be produced by recv and send\n   301→\t\t// Requests channel is unbounded. The Envoy<->XDS Proxy<->Istiod system produces a natural\n   302→\t\t// looping of Recv and Send. Due to backpressure introduced by gRPC natively (that is, Send() can\n   303→\t\t// only send so much data without being Recv'd before it starts blocking), along with the\n   304→\t\t// backpressure provided by our channels, we have a risk of deadlock where both Xdsproxy and\n   305→\t\t// Istiod are trying to Send, but both are blocked by gRPC backpressure until Recv() is called.\n   306→\t\t// However, Recv can fail to be called by Send being blocked. This can be triggered by the two\n   307→\t\t// sources in our system (Envoy request and Istiod pushes) producing more events than we can keep\n   308→\t\t// up with.\n   309→\t\t// See https://github.com/istio/istio/issues/39209 for more information\n   310→\t\t//\n   311→\t\t// To prevent these issues, we need to either:\n   312→\t\t// 1. Apply backpressure directly to Envoy requests or Istiod pushes\n   313→\t\t// 2. Make part of the system unbounded\n   314→\t\t//\n   315→\t\t// (1) is challenging because we cannot do a conditional Recv (for Envoy requests), and changing\n   316→\t\t// the control plane requires substantial changes. Instead, we make the requests channel\n   317→\t\t// unbounded. This is the least likely to cause issues as the messages we store here are the\n   318→\t\t// smallest relative to other channels.\n   319→\t\trequestsChan: channels.NewUnbounded[*discovery.DiscoveryRequest](),\n   320→\t\t// Allow a buffer of 1. This ensures we queue up at most 2 (one in process, 1 pending) responses before forwarding.\n   321→\t\tresponsesChan: make(chan *discovery.DiscoveryResponse, 1),\n   322→\t\tstopChan:      make(chan struct{}),\n   323→\t\tdownstream:    downstream,\n   324→\t}\n   325→\n   326→\tp.registerStream(con)\n   327→\tdefer p.unregisterStream(con)\n   328→\n   329→\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), time.Second*5)\n   330→\tdefer cancel()\n   331→\n   332→\tupstreamConn, err := p.buildUpstreamConn(ctx)\n   333→\tif err != nil {\n   334→\t\tproxyLog.Errorf(\"failed to connect to upstream %s: %v\", p.istiodAddress, err)\n   335→\t\tmetrics.IstiodConnectionFailures.Increment()\n   336→\t\treturn err\n   337→\t}\n   338→\tdefer upstreamConn.Close()\n   339→\n   340→\txds := discovery.NewAggregatedDiscoveryServiceClient(upstreamConn)\n   341→\tctx = metadata.AppendToOutgoingContext(context.Background(), \"ClusterID\", p.clusterID)\n   342→\tfor k, v := range p.xdsHeaders {\n   343→\t\tctx = metadata.AppendToOutgoingContext(ctx, k, v)\n   344→\t}\n   345→\t// We must propagate upstream termination to Envoy. This ensures that we resume the full XDS sequence on new connection\n   346→\treturn p.handleUpstream(ctx, con, xds)\n   347→}\n   348→\n   349→func (p *XdsProxy) buildUpstreamConn(ctx context.Context) (*grpc.ClientConn, error) {\n   350→\tp.optsMutex.RLock()\n   351→\topts := p.dialOptions\n   352→\tp.optsMutex.RUnlock()\n   353→\treturn grpc.DialContext(ctx, p.istiodAddress, opts...)\n   354→}\n   355→\n   356→func (p *XdsProxy) handleUpstream(ctx context.Context, con *ProxyConnection, xds discovery.AggregatedDiscoveryServiceClient) error {\n   357→\tlog := proxyLog.WithLabels(\"id\", con.conID)\n   358→\tupstream, err := xds.StreamAggregatedResources(ctx,\n   359→\t\tgrpc.MaxCallRecvMsgSize(defaultClientMaxReceiveMessageSize))\n   360→\tif err != nil {\n   361→\t\t// Envoy logs errors again, so no need to log beyond debug level\n   362→\t\tlog.Debugf(\"failed to create upstream grpc client: %v\", err)\n   363→\t\t// Increase metric when xds connection error, for example: forgot to restart ingressgateway or sidecar after changing root CA.\n   364→\t\tmetrics.IstiodConnectionErrors.Increment()\n   365→\t\treturn err\n   366→\t}\n   367→\tlog.Infof(\"connected to upstream XDS server: %s\", p.istiodAddress)\n   368→\tdefer log.Debugf(\"disconnected from XDS server: %s\", p.istiodAddress)\n   369→\n   370→\tcon.upstream = upstream\n   371→\n   372→\t// Handle upstream xds recv\n   373→\tgo func() {\n   374→\t\tfor {\n   375→\t\t\t// from istiod\n   376→\t\t\tresp, err := con.upstream.Recv()\n   377→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   378→\t\t\t\tupstreamErr(con, err)\n   379→\t\t\t\treturn\n   380→\t\t\t}\n   381→\t\t\tselect {\n   382→\t\t\tcase con.responsesChan <- resp:\n   383→\t\t\tcase <-con.stopChan:\n   384→\t\t\t}\n   385→\t\t}\n   386→\t}()\n   387→\n   388→\tgo p.handleUpstreamRequest(con)\n   389→\tgo p.handleUpstreamResponse(con)\n   390→\n   391→\tfor {\n   392→\t\tselect {\n   393→\t\tcase err := <-con.upstreamError:\n   394→\t\t\t// error from upstream Istiod.\n   395→\t\t\treturn err\n   396→\t\tcase err := <-con.downstreamError:\n   397→\t\t\t// error from downstream Envoy.\n   398→\t\t\t// On downstream error, we will return. This propagates the error to downstream envoy which will trigger reconnect\n   399→\t\t\treturn err\n   400→\t\tcase <-con.stopChan:\n   401→\t\t\tlog.Debugf(\"upstream stopped\")\n   402→\t\t\treturn nil\n   403→\t\t}\n   404→\t}\n   405→}\n   406→\n   407→func (p *XdsProxy) handleUpstreamRequest(con *ProxyConnection) {\n   408→\tinitialRequestsSent := atomic.NewBool(false)\n   409→\tgo func() {\n   410→\t\tfor {\n   411→\t\t\t// recv xds requests from envoy\n   412→\t\t\treq, err := con.downstream.Recv()\n   413→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   414→\t\t\t\tdownstreamErr(con, err)\n   415→\t\t\t\treturn\n   416→\t\t\t}\n   417→\n   418→\t\t\t// forward to istiod\n   419→\t\t\tcon.sendRequest(req)\n   420→\t\t\tif !initialRequestsSent.Load() && req.TypeUrl == model.ListenerType {\n   421→\t\t\t\t// fire off an initial NDS request\n   422→\t\t\t\tif _, f := p.handlers[model.NameTableType]; f {\n   423→\t\t\t\t\tcon.sendRequest(&discovery.DiscoveryRequest{\n   424→\t\t\t\t\t\tTypeUrl: model.NameTableType,\n   425→\t\t\t\t\t})\n   426→\t\t\t\t}\n   427→\t\t\t\t// fire off an initial PCDS request\n   428→\t\t\t\tif _, f := p.handlers[model.ProxyConfigType]; f {\n   429→\t\t\t\t\tcon.sendRequest(&discovery.DiscoveryRequest{\n   430→\t\t\t\t\t\tTypeUrl: model.ProxyConfigType,\n   431→\t\t\t\t\t})\n   432→\t\t\t\t}\n   433→\t\t\t\t// set flag before sending the initial request to prevent race.\n   434→\t\t\t\tinitialRequestsSent.Store(true)\n   435→\t\t\t\t// Fire of a configured initial request, if there is one\n   436→\t\t\t\tp.connectedMutex.RLock()\n   437→\t\t\t\tinitialRequest := p.initialHealthRequest\n   438→\t\t\t\tif initialRequest != nil {\n   439→\t\t\t\t\tcon.sendRequest(initialRequest)\n   440→\t\t\t\t}\n   441→\t\t\t\tp.connectedMutex.RUnlock()\n   442→\t\t\t}\n   443→\t\t}\n   444→\t}()\n   445→\n   446→\tdefer con.upstream.CloseSend() // nolint\n   447→\tfor {\n   448→\t\tselect {\n   449→\t\tcase req := <-con.requestsChan.Get():\n   450→\t\t\tcon.requestsChan.Load()\n   451→\t\t\tif req.TypeUrl == model.HealthInfoType && !initialRequestsSent.Load() {\n   452→\t\t\t\t// only send healthcheck probe after LDS request has been sent\n   453→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   454→\t\t\t}\n   455→\t\t\tproxyLog.Debugf(\"request for type url %s\", req.TypeUrl)\n   456→\t\t\tmetrics.XdsProxyRequests.Increment()\n   457→\t\t\tif req.TypeUrl == model.ExtensionConfigurationType {\n   458→\t\t\t\tif req.VersionInfo != \"\" {\n   459→\t\t\t\t\tp.ecdsLastAckVersion.Store(req.VersionInfo)\n   460→\t\t\t\t}\n   461→\t\t\t\tp.ecdsLastNonce.Store(req.ResponseNonce)\n   462→\t\t\t}\n   463→\t\t\tif err := con.upstream.Send(req); err != nil {\n   464→\t\t\t\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"send error for type url %s: %v\", req.TypeUrl, err)\n   465→\t\t\t\tupstreamErr(con, err)\n   466→\t\t\t\treturn\n   467→\t\t\t}\n   468→\t\tcase <-con.stopChan:\n   469→\t\t\treturn\n   470→\t\t}\n   471→\t}\n   472→}\n   473→\n   474→func (p *XdsProxy) handleUpstreamResponse(con *ProxyConnection) {\n   475→\tforwardEnvoyCh := make(chan *discovery.DiscoveryResponse, 1)\n   476→\tfor {\n   477→\t\tselect {\n   478→\t\tcase resp := <-con.responsesChan:\n   479→\t\t\t// TODO: separate upstream response handling from requests sending, which are both time costly\n   480→\t\t\tproxyLog.WithLabels(\n   481→\t\t\t\t\"id\", con.conID,\n   482→\t\t\t\t\"type\", model.GetShortType(resp.TypeUrl),\n   483→\t\t\t\t\"resources\", len(resp.Resources),\n   484→\t\t\t).Debugf(\"upstream response\")\n   485→\t\t\tmetrics.XdsProxyResponses.Increment()\n   486→\t\t\tif h, f := p.handlers[resp.TypeUrl]; f {\n   487→\t\t\t\tif len(resp.Resources) == 0 {\n   488→\t\t\t\t\t// Empty response, nothing to do\n   489→\t\t\t\t\t// This assumes internal types are always singleton\n   490→\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n   491→\t\t\t\t}\n   492→\t\t\t\terr := h(resp.Resources[0])\n   493→\t\t\t\tvar errorResp *google_rpc.Status\n   494→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   495→\t\t\t\t\terrorResp = &google_rpc.Status{\n   496→\t\t\t\t\t\tCode:    int32(codes.Internal),\n   497→\t\t\t\t\t\tMessage: err.Error(),\n   498→\t\t\t\t\t}\n   499→\t\t\t\t}\n   500→\t\t\t\t// Send ACK/NACK\n   501→\t\t\t\tcon.sendRequest(&discovery.DiscoveryRequest{\n   502→\t\t\t\t\tVersionInfo:   resp.VersionInfo,\n   503→\t\t\t\t\tTypeUrl:       resp.TypeUrl,\n   504→\t\t\t\t\tResponseNonce: resp.Nonce,\n   505→\t\t\t\t\tErrorDetail:   errorResp,\n   506→\t\t\t\t})\n   507→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   508→\t\t\t}\n   509→\t\t\tswitch resp.TypeUrl {\n   510→\t\t\tcase model.ExtensionConfigurationType:\n   511→\t\t\t\tif features.WasmRemoteLoadConversion {\n   512→\t\t\t\t\t// If Wasm remote load conversion feature is enabled, rewrite and send.\n   513→\t\t\t\t\tgo p.rewriteAndForward(con, resp, func(resp *discovery.DiscoveryResponse) {\n   514→\t\t\t\t\t\t// Forward the response using the thread of `handleUpstreamResponse`\n   515→\t\t\t\t\t\t// to prevent concurrent access to forwardToEnvoy\n   516→\t\t\t\t\t\tselect {\n   517→\t\t\t\t\t\tcase forwardEnvoyCh <- resp:\n   518→\t\t\t\t\t\tcase <-con.stopChan:\n   519→\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n   520→\t\t\t\t\t})\n   521→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   522→\t\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, forward ECDS resource update directly to Envoy.\n   523→\t\t\t\t\tforwardToEnvoy(con, resp)\n   524→\t\t\t\t}\n   525→\t\t\tdefault:\n   526→\t\t\t\tforwardToEnvoy(con, resp)\n   527→\t\t\t}\n   528→\t\tcase resp := <-forwardEnvoyCh:\n   529→\t\t\tforwardToEnvoy(con, resp)\n   530→\t\tcase <-con.stopChan:\n   531→\t\t\treturn\n   532→\t\t}\n   533→\t}\n   534→}\n   535→\n   536→func (p *XdsProxy) rewriteAndForward(con *ProxyConnection, resp *discovery.DiscoveryResponse, forward func(resp *discovery.DiscoveryResponse)) {\n   537→\tif err := wasm.MaybeConvertWasmExtensionConfig(resp.Resources, p.wasmCache); err != nil {\n   538→\t\tproxyLog.Debugf(\"sending NACK for ECDS resources %+v, err: %+v\", resp.Resources, err)\n   539→\t\tcon.sendRequest(&discovery.DiscoveryRequest{\n   540→\t\t\tVersionInfo:   p.ecdsLastAckVersion.Load(),\n   541→\t\t\tTypeUrl:       resp.TypeUrl,\n   542→\t\t\tResponseNonce: resp.Nonce,\n   543→\t\t\tErrorDetail: &google_rpc.Status{\n   544→\t\t\t\tCode:    int32(codes.Internal),\n   545→\t\t\t\tMessage: err.Error(),\n   546→\t\t\t},\n   547→\t\t})\n   548→\t\treturn\n   549→\t}\n   550→\tproxyLog.Debugf(\"forward ECDS resources %+v\", resp.Resources)\n   551→\tforward(resp)\n   552→}\n   553→\n   554→func forwardToEnvoy(con *ProxyConnection, resp *discovery.DiscoveryResponse) {\n   555→\tif !model.IsEnvoyType(resp.TypeUrl) && resp.TypeUrl != model.WorkloadType {\n   556→\t\tproxyLog.Errorf(\"Skipping forwarding type url %s to Envoy as is not a valid Envoy type\", resp.TypeUrl)\n   557→\t\treturn\n   558→\t}\n   559→\tif con.isClosed() {\n   560→\t\tproxyLog.WithLabels(\"id\", con.conID).Errorf(\"downstream dropped xds push to Envoy, connection already closed\")\n   561→\t\treturn\n   562→\t}\n   563→\tif err := sendDownstream(con.downstream, resp); err != nil {\n   564→\t\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"send error for type url %s: %v\", resp.TypeUrl, err)\n   565→\t\tdownstreamErr(con, err)\n   566→\t\treturn\n   567→\t}\n   568→}\n   569→\n   570→// sendDownstream sends discovery response.\n   571→func sendDownstream(downstream adsStream, response *discovery.DiscoveryResponse) error {\n   572→\ttStart := time.Now()\n   573→\tdefer func() {\n   574→\t\t// This is a hint to help debug slow responses.\n   575→\t\tif time.Since(tStart) > 10*time.Second {\n   576→\t\t\tproxyLog.Warnf(\"sendDownstream took %v\", time.Since(tStart))\n   577→\t\t}\n   578→\t}()\n   579→\treturn downstream.Send(response)\n   580→}\n   581→\n   582→func (p *XdsProxy) close() {\n   583→\tclose(p.stopChan)\n   584→\tp.wasmCache.Cleanup()\n   585→\tif p.downstreamGrpcServer != nil {\n   586→\t\tp.downstreamGrpcServer.Stop()\n   587→\t}\n   588→\tif p.downstreamListener != nil {\n   589→\t\t_ = p.downstreamListener.Close()\n   590→\t}\n   591→}\n   592→\n   593→func (p *XdsProxy) initDownstreamServer() error {\n   594→\tl, err := uds.NewListener(p.xdsUdsPath)\n   595→\tif err != nil {\n   596→\t\treturn err\n   597→\t}\n   598→\t// TODO: Expose keepalive options to agent cmd line flags.\n   599→\topts := p.downstreamGrpcOptions\n   600→\topts = append(opts, istiogrpc.ServerOptions(istiokeepalive.DefaultOption(), xdspkg.RecordRecvSize)...)\n   601→\tgrpcs := grpc.NewServer(opts...)\n   602→\tdiscovery.RegisterAggregatedDiscoveryServiceServer(grpcs, p)\n   603→\treflection.Register(grpcs)\n   604→\tp.downstreamGrpcServer = grpcs\n   605→\tp.downstreamListener = l\n   606→\treturn nil\n   607→}\n   608→\n   609→func (p *XdsProxy) k.Name\n    52→}\n    53→\n    54→type keySet = sets.Set[resourceKey]\n    55→\n    56→// resourceNode represents a resource state in the dynamic tree structure of the service mesh.\n    57→// It tracks the relationships of a resource with its parents and children within the mesh.\n    58→//\n    59→// Example: Consider a scenario where we have a direct wildcard CDS watch.\n    60→// Upon receiving a response, suppose some CDS resources named A, B, etc., are added. The resulting tree structure would be:\n    61→//\n    62→//\tCDS/*:\n    63→//\t  CDS/A:\n    64→//\t  CDS/B:\n    65→//\n    66→// In this case, CDS/A and CDS/B are nodes under the wildcard CDS watch.\n    67→//\n    68→// Further, if we register a dependency on an EDS resource named C for CDS added resources,\n    69→// the tree expands to:\n    70→//\n    71→//\tCDS/*:\n    72→//\t  CDS/A:\n    73→//\t    EDS/C:\n    74→//\t  CDS/B:\n    75→//\t    EDS/C:\n    76→//\n    77→// Here, CDS/A and CDS/B become parents of EDS/C, and EDS/C is a child of both CDS/A and CDS/B.\n    78→//\n    79→// If a response later indicates that the CDS resource A is removed, all relationships originating from A are also removed.\n    80→// The updated tree would then be:\n    81→//\n    82→//\tCDS/*:\n    83→//\t  CDS/B:\n    84→//\t    EDS/C:\n    85→//\n    86→// This change reflects the removal of CDS/A and its associated child link to EDS/C.\n    87→type resourceNode struct {\n    88→\t// Parents of the resource. If nil, this is explicitly watched\n    89→\tParents keySet\n    90→\t// Children of the resource\n    91→\tChildren keySet\n    92→}\n    93→\n    94→type HandlerContext interface {\n    95→\tRegisterDependency(typeURL string, resourceName ...string)\n    96→\tReject(reason error)\n    97→}\n    98→\n    99→var _ HandlerContext = &handlerContext{}\n   100→\n   101→// HandlerContext provides an event for a single delta response, allowing handlers to react to it.\n   102→// Operations done in the handler may be batched together with other handler's.\n   103→type handlerContext struct {\n   104→\tsub  keySet\n   105→\tnack error\n   106→}\n   107→\n   108→func (h *handlerContext) RegisterDependency(typeURL string, resourceName ...string) {\n   109→\tif h.sub == nil {\n   110→\t\th.sub = make(keySet)\n   111→\t}\n   112→\tfor _, r := range resourceName {\n   113→\t\tkey := resourceKey{\n   114→\t\t\tName:    r,\n   115→\t\t\tTypeURL: typeURL,\n   116→\t\t}\n   117→\t\th.sub.Insert(key)\n   118→\t}\n   119→}\n   120→\n   121→func (h *handlerContext) Reject(reason error) {\n   122→\th.nack = reason\n   123→}\n   124→\n   125→// DeltaADSConfig for delta ADS connection.\n   126→type DeltaADSConfig struct {\n   127→\tConfig\n   128→}\n   129→\n   130→type Resource struct {\n   131→\tName    string\n   132→\tVersion string\n   133→\tEntity  proto.Message\n   134→}\n   135→\n   136→type HandlerFunc func(ctx HandlerContext, res *Resource, event Event)\n   137→\n   138→// Client is a stateful ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) client designed to handle delta updates from an xDS server.\n   139→// Central to this client is a dynamic 'tree' of resources, representing the relationships and states of resources in the service mesh.\n   140→// The client's operation unfolds in the following steps:\n   141→//\n   142→//  1. Sending Initial Requests: The client initiates requests for resources it needs, as specified by the Watch function.\n   143→//     This step sets the stage for receiving relevant DeltaDiscoveryResponse from the server.\n   144→//\n   145→//  2. Processing DeltaDiscoveryResponses: Upon receiving a delta response, the client performs several key actions:\n   146→//     - Event Handling: Triggers specific handlers for each resource, as register using Register function during client initialization.\n   147→//     - Tree Update: Modifies its 'tree' to reflect changes in resources, such as adding new resources,\n   148→//     updating relationships between parents and children, and removing or unlinking resources.\n   149→//\n   150→//  3. State Synchronization: Post-processing the delta response, the client updates its internal state. This involves:\n   151→//     - Acknowledgements and Errors: Communicating acknowledgements or errors back to the server based on the\n   152→//     processing outcome. In cases of error or rejection, a Nack can be sent using HandlerContext.Reject.\n   153→//     - Dependency Updates: Triggering requests for dependent resources. These dependencies are established via\n   154→//     HandlerContext.RegisterDependency.\n   155→//\n   156→// An example of a handler registration is as follows:\n   157→//\n   158→//\tclusterHandler := Register(func(ctx HandlerContext, res *cluster.Cluster, event Event) {\n   159→//\t  if event == EventDelete {\n   160→//\t    return\n   161→//\t  }\n   162→//\t  ctx.RegisterDependency(v3.SecretType, ExtractClusterSecretResources(t, res)...)\n   163→//\t  ctx.RegisterDependency(v3.EndpointType, ExtractEdsClusterNames([]*cluster.Cluster{res})...)\n   164→//\t})\n   165→//\n   166→// It means that when a cluster is added or updated, the client will trigger requests for the\n   167→// secrets and endpoints that the cluster depends on.\n   168→//\n   169→// An example of register handlers:\n   170→//\n   171→//\thandlers := []Option{\n   172→//\t  clusterHandler,\n   173→//\t  Watch[*cluster.Cluster](\"*\"),\n   174→//\t  listenerHandler,\n   175→//\t  Watch[*listener.Listener](\"*\"),\n   176→//\t  endpointsHandler,\n   177→//\t  routesHandler,\n   178→//\t  secretsHandler,\n   179→//\t}\n   180→//\n   181→// client := NewDelta(\"localhost:8080\", handlers...)\n   182→//\n   183→// It means that the client will watch all clusters and listeners, and trigger resource events for\n   184→// clusters, listeners, endpoints, routes and secrets that the clusters and listeners depend on.\n   185→type Client struct {\n   186→\tlog *log.Scope\n   187→\n   188→\tcfg      *DeltaADSConfig\n   189→\thandlers map[string]HandlerFunc\n   190→\t// tree is a map where each key is a `resourceKey` (comprising the resource name and typeURL)\n   191→\t// and each added resource is a `resourceNode`. This tree structure represents the dynamic state\n   192→\t// and relationships of resources.\n   193→\ttree map[resourceKey]resourceNode\n   194→\n   195→\txdsClient DeltaAggregatedResourcesClient\n   196→\tconn      *grpc.ClientConn\n   197→\n   198→\t// initialWatches is the list of resources we are watching on startup\n   199→\tinitialWatches []resourceKey\n   200→\n   201→\t// initialWatches is a list of resources we were initially watching and have not yet received\n   202→\tpendingWatches sets.Set[resourceKey]\n   203→\t// synced is used to indicate the initial watches have all been seen\n   204→\tsynced chan struct{}\n   205→\n   206→\t// sendNodeMeta is set to true if the connection is new - and we need to send node meta\n   207→\tsendNodeMeta bool\n   208→\n   209→\t// lastReceivedNonce nonce, by type\n   210→\tlastReceivedNonce map[string]string\n   211→\n   212→\t// errChan is used to signal errors from the delta stream\n   213→\terrChan chan error\n   214→\n   215→\t// closed is set to true when the client is closed\n   216→\tclosed *atomic.Bool\n   217→}\n   218→\n   219→func (c *Client) trigger(ctx *handlerContext, typeURL string, r *discovery.Resource, event Event) error {\n   220→\tvar res *Resource\n   221→\tif r == nil {\n   222→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"triggered by event %d,but resource is nil\", event)\n   223→\t}\n   224→\tif event == EventAdd {\n   225→\t\tif r.Resource == nil {\n   226→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"triggered by EventAdd,but be added resource object is nil\")\n   227→\t\t}\n   228→\t\tentity := newProto(typeURL)\n   229→\t\tif entity == nil {\n   230→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"new resource entity by typeURL: %s error\", entity)\n   231→\t\t}\n   232→\t\tif err := r.Resource.UnmarshalTo(entity); err != nil {\n   233→\t\t\treturn err\n   234→\t\t}\n   235→\t\tres = &Resource{\n   236→\t\t\tName:    r.Name,\n   237→\t\t\tVersion: r.Version,\n   238→\t\t\tEntity:  entity,\n   239→\t\t}\n   240→\t} else {\n   241→\t\t// EventDelete\n   242→\t\tres = &Resource{\n   243→\t\t\tName: r.Name,\n   244→\t\t}\n   245→\t}\n   246→\thandler, f := c.handlers[typeURL]\n   247→\tif !f {\n   248→\t\tc.log.Warnf(\"ignoring unknown type %v\", typeURL)\n   249→\t\treturn nil\n   250→\t}\n   251→\thandler(ctx, res, event)\n   252→\treturn nil\n   253→}\n   254→\n   255→// getProtoMessageType returns the Golang type of the proto with the specified name.\n   256→func newProto(tt string) proto.Message {\n   257→\tname := protoreflect.FullName(strings.TrimPrefix(tt, pm.APITypePrefix))\n   258→\tt, err := protoregistry.GlobalTypes.FindMessageByName(name)\n   259→\tif err != nil || t == nil {\n   260→\t\treturn nil\n   261→\t}\n   262→\treturn t.New().Interface()\n   263→}\n   264→\n   265→// Run starts the client. If a backoffPolicy is configured, it will reconnect on error.\n   266→func (c *Client) Run(ctx context.Context) {\n   267→\tc.runWithReconnects(ctx)\n   268→}\n   269→\n   270→// Synced returns a runOnce(ctx context.Context) error {\n   276→\tif err := c.dial(ctx); err != nil {\n   277→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"dial fail: %v\", err)\n   278→\t}\n   279→\tdefer c.conn.Close()\n   280→\n   281→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n   282→\tdefer cancel()\n   283→\txds := discovery.NewAggregatedDiscoveryServiceClient(c.conn)\n   284→\txdsClient, err := xds.DeltaAggregatedResources(ctx, grpc.MaxCallRecvMsgSize(math.MaxInt32))\n   285→\tif err != nil {\n   286→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delta stream: %v\", err)\n   287→\t}\n   288→\tc.log.WithLabels(\"node\", c.nodeID()).Infof(\"established connection\")\n   289→\tc.sendNodeMeta = true\n   290→\tc.xdsClient = xdsClient\n   291→\tfor _, w := range c.initialWatches {\n   292→\t\tc.log.Infof(\"sending initial watch %v\", w.TypeURL)\n   293→\t\tif err := c.request(w); err != nil {\n   294→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"initial watch: %v\", err)\n   295→\t\t}\n   296→\t}\n   297→\treturn c.handleRecv()\n   298→}\n   299→\n   300→func (c *Client) dial(ctx context.Context) error {\n   301→\tif c.conn != nil {\n   302→\t\t_ = c.conn.Close()\n   303→\t}\n   304→\tconn, err := dialWithConfig(ctx, &c.cfg.Config)\n   305→\tif err != nil {\n   306→\t\treturn err\n   307→\t}\n   308→\tc.conn = conn\n   309→\treturn nil\n   310→}\n   311→\n   312→// runWithReconnects will create a new stream and schedule a retry once disconnected\n   313→func (c *Client) runWithReconnects(ctx context.Context) {\n   314→\tfor {\n   315→\t\tif c.closed.Load() {\n   316→\t\t\tbreak\n   317→\t\t}\n   318→\t\terr := c.runOnce(ctx)\n   319→\t\tif c.cfg.BackoffPolicy == nil {\n   320→\t\t\tlog.Warnf(\"disconnected: %v\", err)\n   321→\t\t\tbreak\n   322→\t\t}\n   323→\t\tnext := c.cfg.BackoffPolicy.NextBackOff()\n   324→\t\tc.log.Warnf(\"disconnected, retrying in %v: %v\", next, err)\n   325→\t\tif !sleep.UntilContext(ctx, next) {\n   326→\t\t\tc.log.Warnf(\"context canceled (%v), not retrying again: %v\", context.Cause(ctx), err)\n   327→\t\t\tbreak\n   328→\t\t}\n   329→\t}\n   330→\tc.closed.Store(true)\n   331→}\n   332→\n   333→type Option func(c *Client)\n   334→\n   335→func NewDelta(discoveryAddr string, config *DeltaADSConfig, opts ...Option) *Client {\n   336→\tif config == nil {\n   337→\t\tconfig = &DeltaADSConfig{}\n   338→\t}\n   339→\tconfig.Address = discoveryAddr\n   340→\tconfig.Config = setDefaultConfig(&config.Config)\n   341→\tc := &Client{\n   342→\t\tlog:               deltaLog.WithLabels(\"target\", ptr.NonEmptyOrDefault(config.ClientName,       make(chan error, 10),\n   347→\t\tsynced:            make(chan struct{}),\n   348→\t\tpendingWatches:    sets.New[resourceKey](),\n   349→\t\tlastReceivedNonce: map[string]string{},\n reflected by the proto message.\n   373→func Register[T proto.Message](f func(ctx HandlerContext, resourceName string, resourceVersion string, resourceEntity T, event Event)) Option {\n   374→\treturn func(c *Client) {\n   375→\t\tc.handlers[typeName[T]()] = func(ctx HandlerContext, res *Resource, event Event) {\n   376→\t\t\tif res.Entity == nil {\n   377→\t\t\t\tvar nilEntity T\n   378→\t\t\t\tf(ctx, res.Name, res.Version, nilEntity, event)\n   379→\t\t\t} else {\n   380→\t\t\t\tf(ctx, res.Name, res.Version, res.Entity.(T), event)\n   381→\t\t\t}\n   382→\t\t}\n   383→\t}\n   384→}\n   385→\n   386→// Watch registers an initial watch for a type based on the type reflected by the proto message.\n   387→func Watch[T proto.Message](resourceName string) Option {\n   388→\treturn initWatch(typeName[T](), resourceName)\n   389→}\n   390→\n   391→func initWatch(typeURL string, resourceName string) Option {\n   392→\treturn func(c *Client) {\n   393→\t\tif resourceName == \"*\" {\n   394→\t\t\t// Normalize to allow both forms\n   395→\t\t\tresourceName = \"\"\n   396→\t\t}\n   397→\t\tkey := resourceKey{\n   398→\t\t\tName:    resourceName,\n   399→\t\t\tTypeURL: typeURL,\n   400→\t\t}\n   401→\t\texisting, f := c.tree[key]\n   402→\t\tif f {\n   403→\t\t\t// We are watching directly now, so erase any parents\n   404→\t\t\texisting.Parents = nil\n   405→\t\t\texisting.Children = nil\n   406→\t\t} else {\n   407→\t\t\tc.tree[key] = resourceNode{\n   408→\t\t\t\tParents:  make(keySet),\n   409→\t\t\t\tChildren: make(keySet),\n error {\n   418→\thasSucceeded := false\n   419→\tfor {\n   420→\t\tmsg, err := c.xdsClient.Recv()\n   421→\t\tif err != nil {\n   422→\t\t\treturn err\n   423→\t\t}\n   424→\t\tc.log.WithLabels(\"type\", msg.TypeUrl, \"size\", len(msg.Resources), \"removes\", len(msg.RemovedResources)).Infof(\"received response\")\n   425→\t\tif err := c.handleDeltaResponse(msg); err != nil {\n   426→\t\t\tc.log.WithLabels(\"type\", msg.TypeUrl).Infof(\"handle response failed: %v\", err)\n   427→\t\t\tif err2 := c.xdsClient.CloseSend(); err2 != nil {\n   428→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to close connection (%v) in response to: %v\", err2, err)\n   429→\t\t\t}\n   430→\t\t\treturn err\n   431→\t\t}\n   432→\t\tif !hasSucceeded && c.cfg.BackoffPolicy != nil {\n   433→\t\t\t// We succeeded once, so reset\n   434→\t\t\thasSucceeded = true\n   435→\t\t\tc.cfg.BackoffPolicy.Reset()\n   436→\t\t}\n   437→\t\tc.lastReceivedNonce[msg.TypeUrl] = msg.Nonce\n   438→\t}\n   439→}\n   440→\n   441→func (c *Client) handleDeltaResponse(d *discovery.DeltaDiscoveryResponse) error {\n   442→\tvar rejects []error\n   443→\tallAdds := map[string]sets.Set[string]{}\n   444→\tallRemoves := map[string]sets.Set[string]{}\n   445→\tctx := &handlerContext{}\n   446→\tif isDebugType(d.TypeUrl) {\n   447→\t\t// No need to ack and type check for debug types\n   448→\t\treturn nil\n   449→\t}\n   450→\n   451→\tc.markReceived(resourceKey{\n   452→\t\tName:    \"\", // If they did a wildcard sub\n   453→\t\tTypeURL: d.TypeUrl,\n   454→\t})\n   455→\tfor _, r := range d.Resources {\n   456→\t\tif d.TypeUrl != r.Resource.TypeUrl {\n   457→\t\t\tc.log.Errorf(\"Invalid response: mismatch of type url: %v vs %v\", d.TypeUrl, r.Resource.TypeUrl)\n   458→\t\t\tcontinue\n   459→\t\t}\n   460→\t\terr := c.trigger(ctx, d.TypeUrl, r, EventAdd)\n   461→\t\tif err != nil {\n   462→\t\t\treturn err\n   463→\t\t}\n   464→\t\tparentKey := resourceKey{\n   465→\t\t\tName:    r.Name,\n   466→\t\t\tTypeURL: r.Resource.TypeUrl,\n   467→\t\t}\n   468→\t\tc.markReceived(parentKey)\n   469→\t\tc.establishResource(parentKey)\n   470→\t\tif ctx.nack != nil {\n   471→\t\t\trejects = append(rejects, ctx.nack)\n   472→\t\t\t// On NACK, do not apply resource changes\n   473→\t\t\tcontinue\n   474→\t\t}\n   475→\n   476→\t\tremove, add := c.tree[parentKey].Children.Diff(ctx.sub)\n   477→\t\tfor _, key := range add {\n   478→\t\t\tsets.InsertOrNew(allAdds, key.TypeURL, key.Name)\n   479→\t\t\tc.relate(parentKey, key)\n   480→\t\t}\n   481→\t\tfor _, key := range remove {\n   482→\t\t\tsets.InsertOrNew(allRemoves, key.TypeURL, key.Name)\n   483→\t\t\tc.unrelate(parentKey, key)\n   484→\t\t}\n   485→\t}\n   486→\tfor _, r := range d.RemovedResources {\n   487→\t\tkey := resourceKey{\n   488→\t\t\tName:    r,\n   489→\t\t\tTypeURL: d.TypeUrl,\n   490→\t\t}\n   491→\t\tremoved := &discovery.Resource{\n   492→\t\t\tName: r,\n   493→\t\t}\n   494→\t\terr := c.trigger(ctx, d.TypeUrl, removed, EventDelete)\n   495→\t\tif err != nil {\n   496→\t\t\treturn err\n   497→\t\t}\n   498→\n   499→\t\tsets.InsertOrNew(allRemoves, key.TypeURL, key.Name)\n   500→\t\tc.drop(key)\n   501→\t}\n   502→\tif err := c.send(resourceKey{TypeURL: d.TypeUrl}, d.Nonce, joinError(rejects)); err != nil {\n   503→\t\treturn err\n   504→\t}\n   505→\tfor t, sub := range allAdds {\n   506→\t\tunsub, f := allRemoves[t]\n   507→\t\tif f {\n   508→\t\t\tdelete(allRemoves, t)\n   509→\t\t}\n   510→\t\tc.update(t, sub, unsub, d)\n   511→\t}\n   512→\treturn nil\n   513→}\n   514→\n   515→func (c *Client) markReceived(k resourceKey) {\n   516→\tif c.pendingWatches.Contains(k) {\n   517→\t\tc.pendingWatches.Delete(k)\n   518→\t\tif
